properties\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cdiv\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eThe Act Amending the Revenue Code No. 53 B.E. 2564 (2021) (“e-Service Tax Law”) regarding value added tax (“VAT”) collection by foreign electronic service providers who provide services to non-VAT registrants in Thailand was published in the Royal Gazette on the 10th February 2021, to take effect starting 1\u003csup\u003est\u003c/sup\u003e September 2021. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eAs a company registered in Singapore providing electronic service to Thai consumers, Agoda is required to register under the e-Service Tax Law. Under the Act, Agoda is required to remit 7% VAT on amounts earned from Thai consumers to the Thai Revenue Department.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003e“Thai consumer” refers to a “service recipient who is non-VAT registered in Thailand”.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eUnder the VAT Act: \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cspan\u003eIf you are VAT registered, there should be no impact on you. The e-Service Tax Law confirms that you continue to have an obligation to self-assess 7% VAT on commission earned by Agoda. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cspan\u003eIf you are \u003cstrong\u003enot \u003c/strong\u003eVAT registered, i.e. you will be considered a “Thai consumer” and Agoda would apply\u003cs\u003e \u003c/s\u003e 7% VAT on commissions earned from you and remit such amounts to the Thai Revenue Department.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003e \u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003ch3 id=\"h_01F7B66R8DMWPCNBAZDS6B701X\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue110\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-font-size-x-large\"\u003eHow can you update your VAT ID\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThree options are available for you to add your VAT ID:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOption 1. Simply put in the VAT ID through YCS Pop -up\u003c/strong\u003e. On Tuesday 25th May 2021, YCS Pop up V.2 was launched with the ability to let you submit your VAT ID in the correct 13 digit format.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can update your VAT ID at any time in YCS Setting --\u0026gt; Property Settings --\u0026gt; Property Information --\u0026gt; Additional regional settings --\u0026gt; Click save.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://engage.agoda.com/hc/article_attachments/1500019569682/mceclip1.png\" alt=\"mceclip1.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://engage.agoda.com/hc/article_attachments/1500019569702/mceclip2.png\" alt=\"mceclip2.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOption 2. abroad\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eShorter duration bookings are possible for customers awaiting results of COVID test before leaving country, and frontline workers who are employed in an area far from their home and stay in quarantine hotels\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOnly single occupancy is allowed per room, except for the adult companion is allowed)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThere will be no minimum length of stay setting applied to the BLT page\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt may be possible to The standard requirements are below:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCurrently, packages must offer:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e 15 nights minimum stay          \u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e  3 meals a day\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e  Private car transfer from either Don Mueang Airport or Suvarnabhumi Airport\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e  A nurse on call 24/7 and health check-ups\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e  COVID-19 tests that usually take place on the 5th and 13th day of the stay\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e  Hospital transfer if needed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt may be possible to include additional benefits in your package, such as complimentary welcome minibar (with no alcohol), yoga mats or gym materials, extra meals (e.g. afternoon tea), free consultation with doctors, and other items that will make the quarantine stay more comfortable for your guest.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue110\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBooking flow for ASQ bookings\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt is important to note that confirming ASQ bookings require additional steps. guests \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eDuring the spread of the COVID-19 pandemic, we’ve seen a shift in bookings to move towards properties with higher cleanliness scores. The research revealed that cleanliness information will carry on being an important aspect travelers look for in the new normal style of living.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAs a property owner, it’s crucial to showcase the cleanliness related measures you take at your property to build guests’ confidence and enhance their decision when booking. Your goal is to make guests feel confident that their stay will be as safe, clean, and comfortable as in their own homes. Our goal is to make it easy for you to show guests all the measures you’re taking to respond to the pandemic.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1\u003e\u003cspan protocol\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eArranging training to ensure property staff is aligned on the measures, safety, and health protocols e.g. wearing masks, understanding how to handle guests with risks.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eContactless check-in/check-out\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOnline, auto, or self-service check-in to reduce human contact to avoid cross infection.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eTemperature check for guests and required to wear face shield and/or masks at your property.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eSterilizing equipment payment as an alternative option, if possible.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eShow guests what measures you’re taking on posters, TV, etc., throughout your property.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInstall hand sanitizing stations located in high-traffic areas throughout the hotel, such as the front desk, breakfast area, elevator lobbies, and fitness center.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDisplaying cleanliness are the facilities most guests look for nowadays?","title":"What are the facilities most guests look for nowadays?","source_locale":"en-us","locale":"en-us","outdated":false,"outdated_locales":[],"edited_at":"2020-11-25T03:43:50Z","user_segment_id":null,"permission_group_id":311767,"content_tag_ids":[],"label_names":["facility","amenity"],"body":"\u003ctable overview of what facilities are most important to those booking on Agoda today. By learning the priorities of current travelers, you can design or improve your property to meet these needs and attract more bookings. \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan data-contrast=\"none\"\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan data-ccp-props='{\"134233117\":true,\"134233118\":true,\"201341983\":0,\"335559740\":240}'\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\" aria-level=\"1\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eContent \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003cspan data-contrast=\"none\"\u003eThis article includes\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\n\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ3SV8JMZAKH673TYMPZ46\" target=\"_self\"\u003eThe facilities most guests look for\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ3YC2YFD5WRW8XDGJ1FRA\" target=\"_self\"\u003eFast \u0026amp; free Wi-Fi access \u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ44GH0M730GME22EH53WV\" target=\"_self\"\u003eFree breakfast\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ4A99H9CE3DNF3G2PYPK5\" target=\"_self\"\u003eWellness facilities\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ4FYHXPZW39N85CT0SNXR\" target=\"_self\"\u003eSmart entertainment devices\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ4N9WCXXYYWJQJ5F5NDSB\" target=\"_self\"\u003eIn-room food and beverages\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EQYQ4SQ9CM09RBAC5TQGE9E9\" target=\"_self\"\u003eCleanliness facilities\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\" aria-level=\"1\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EQYQ3SV8JMZAKH673TYMPZ46\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eThe facilities most guests look for\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWith millions of daily travelers visiting and booking on Agoda’s website and app, we’ve acquired a huge amount of data that can tell us a lot about what kinds of properties get booked the most. \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccording to our data, the most important facilities to offer to travelers are the following. Make sure that your property offers all or most of them!  \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ3YC2YFD5WRW8XDGJ1FRA\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFast \u0026amp; free Wi-Fi access \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhether on a business trip or on vacation, wi-fi that works is the by far the most important thing to the greatest number of modern travelers. Staying connected with loved ones, uploading and downloading work, and accessing social media and news is so important that poor Wi-Fi is one of the biggest causes of negative reviews. Travelers also use the internet to research their next day trip or meal while traveling.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWi-Fi should be fast and able to work perfectly even at maximum hotel capacity when almost every single guest is connected to the network. Your system needs to scale to handle full capacity or more – such as when you have events with guests who may not even be staying in your rooms.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe signal must be strong in all public areas, as well as in all rooms, whether they are located on the ground floor or on the top floor of the hotel. Travelers now use social media networks for video calls and phone calls, and might be moving around your property while doing so. A dropped signal or call at an important time creates a very bad guest experience.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWi-Fi should be free to those who eat in your restaurants as well, even if they are staying in rooms.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ44GH0M730GME22EH53WV\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFree breakfast \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBreakfast is not only the most important meal of the day, but it is also one the most important services for guests when staying at a hotel because it saves them time and effort on their precious travel days.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eConsider offering a complimentary breakfast for your guests, and make it as tasty and varied as possible. Even if you have to raise your room prices slightly to cover your costs, the perceived value of a free breakfast is usually greater than that of a slightly cheaper room.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ4A99H9CE3DNF3G2PYPK5\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWellness facilities \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWellness travel, or travel associated with the pursuit of maintaining or enhancing one’s personal well-being, is a fast-growing segment that creates $639 billion for the tourism industry.\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-purple\"\u003e* \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAs more consumers adopt wellness as part of their value system, they will increasingly filter their travel experiences through a holistic wellness lens. While traveling, they want to relax, but also to be able to maintain their daily routines, which may require certain facilities:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eWorkout\u003c/strong\u003e facilities such as a pool or fitness center.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eRelaxation and beauty\u003c/strong\u003e facilities such as massage, spa, salon, or sauna.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eMind and body\u003c/strong\u003e facilities such as yoga room or a space for quiet meditation.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eHealthy eating\u003c/strong\u003e food options such as vegan, gluten-free, low-sugar, or plant-based.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eEco and adventure\u003c/strong\u003e activities such as surfing lessons, canoeing, skiing, hiking, or other activities that engage the local environment.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo help you promote your offerings, key wellness activities that you offer will be prominently displayed under your property name on the Agoda property page.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-font-size-small wysiwyg-color-purple\"\u003e\u003cem\u003e*Global Wellness Tourism Economy research by the Global Wellness Institute\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"wysiwyg-text-align-center\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360100703133/mceclip0.png\" alt=\"mceclip0.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ4FYHXPZW39N85CT0SNXR\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSmart entertainment devices \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eSmart TV\u003c/strong\u003e: Netflix and other digital platforms have become a daily habit for a big part of the world, especially for millennials. Allowing guests to connect their devices and watch the rest of the movie they began watching during their flight or catch the latest episode from their favorite series is a plus. Make sure your TVs have either built-in apps like Netflix, or HDMI and USB ports that allow guests to play their own content from their laptops or USB drives.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eBluetooth speakers\u003c/strong\u003e that allow guests to connect to their playlist from smartphones using iTunes or Spotify or other music services. By allowing guests to create their own musical ambience, they can customize their stay. Make sure that your Wi-Fi can handle many guests at once using music streaming services!\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ4N9WCXXYYWJQJ5F5NDSB\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIn-room food and beverages\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eCoffee/Tea maker\u003c/strong\u003e: Offer your guests a cup of quality coffee from the comfort of their room to start their day, without having to order it via room service. For a truly boutique touch, a sleek capsule espresso machine adds a quality impression, with a certain number of free capsules provided per day. A lower cost option is to offer a drip coffee machine, or just hot water makers that can be poured over one-serving coffee drip packets. Whatever you do, don’t offer only instant coffee packets. For most coffee drinkers, instant coffee is so unpalatable that they would rather have nothing at all.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EQYQ4SQ9CM09RBAC5TQGE9E9\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCleanliness facilities \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePrioritizing cleanliness has become the “new normal” way of travel for everyone due to the 2020 COVID-19 pandemic. Guests want to know about the cleanliness measures you take before booking your property.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo improve guest confidence in your property when booking, you should provide cleanliness and hygiene facilities at your hotels that can be displayed prominently in your property content.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRead more about cleanliness facilities and how you can display Humans are visually stimulated – we use pictures to help us select everything we buy, eat, and do. Your presentation of your property and its rooms on Agoda is more than just a catalog – they entice our millions of daily visitors to integrate your place into their travel dreams. It’s important that you offer thorough, inviting, and accurate photos of what your property offers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EK9DW9ZTSYS3G0T8JQ7PJD49\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGet your property photo-ready\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen preparing your hotel for a photo shoot, go a step further than your usual standard in your cleaning routine. The camera will pick up even the slightest detail, so make sure everything is spotless. Arrange every item of furniture and even small objects in their optimal place. See below for specific tips for each room.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360092050194/mceclip0.png\" alt=\"mceclip1.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EK9DWE8S1C32MFCJEHXFQNKR\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePreparing a guest room\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClean, steam, or press linens and fluff pillows\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSteam curtains and keep them open for natural light and view\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClose sheer curtains to create a soft diffuse light, or open sheer curtains if the view is more interesting\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLeave out unsightly objects like air vents or trash cans\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure windows, mirrors, and floors are spotless\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTurn off the TV and hide any wires or cables\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EK9DWK0GFXCF6M5R46QDYB4H\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePreparing a bathroom\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAlways lower toilet seats\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eA full roll of toilet paper makes it seem like it was recently cleaned\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure sinks, showers and baths are not wet\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOpen shower curtains if possible so travelers can get the full picture\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTowels that are hanging or folded should be of equal lengths\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEmpty the trash bins\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eArrange complimentary toiletries in a prominent place so they stand out\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EK9DWS287FZKG7GTD9DZ7ETB\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePreparing a dining area in a restaurant\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChoose food and drinks to be featured in the shoot such as signature dish or drinks\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFood and drinks with a pop of color and creative presentation will look best in photos\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTry to use food that is representative of the restaurant’s signature cuisine\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSet tables and chairs in proper order\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor formal settings, aim for orderliness and perfection\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor casual settings aim for inviting appearance and comfort\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EK9DWX182JKXAYDWHPWYWPKD\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePreparing property facilities\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCommunicate with housekeeping to do a final check before the shoot\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRemove any unnecessary objects like newspaper and magazines\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure all areas are free of guests’ belongings\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePlan your shoot during off-peak hours or when facilities are closed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInform guests in advance that a photoshoot will be taking place as certain facilities, such as the gym, pool, or spa, may need to be closed for guests in order to be photographed properly.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EK9DX1GHGQ2GW2KBSZF1MMP5\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat to avoid when taking photos?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRoad signs or parked cars\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePeople or animals\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOther companies’ logos\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSeasonal decorations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUnsightly objects such as dirty/messy facilities\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePoorly lit scenes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIdentical images were taken at a different angle\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMisleading images of area landmarks or views that you cannot see from the property\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EK9DX6BC8VP925DZBM2CP8YR\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eShooting tips\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eUse a tripod \u003c/strong\u003efor steady, balanced photos. Tripods prevent motion blur while allowing you maximum freedom to make adjustments to composition. You can set your frame, and then make adjustments or furnishings, lighting, or object arrangement without losing your original composition.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eGet the lighting right. \u003c/strong\u003eNatural light is usually the best, but depending on how much natural light you can get in a room or space, you may need to supplement with indoor lighting. Experiment with different lighting combinations in the same composition to find the ideal solution. Play around with how lights hit in the space and don’t be afraid to take a lot of shots to compare. Curtains and blinds should always be open, but sheer curtains can be closed if they create a soft diffuse light, and if the view out the windows does not add value.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eThe composition is key \u003c/strong\u003eto create depth and dynamism in your photos. Shooting from corners makes rooms look larger, and helps a viewer take in the entire space. If you are shooting directly into space from one side, try and make the horizontal lines perfectly flat, top creates a sense of foundation and evenness.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eUse the widest setting on your lens\u003c/strong\u003e to capture more room space in the shot, making rooms and open spaces appear wider and more generous.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eMix up your shots. \u003c/strong\u003eNot only a wide variety of shots but also a wide variety of styles will make your property seem like a dynamic and diverse place. For example, classic wide-angle or panoramic shots set the scene and enable guests to imagine themselves within the hotel. By pairing these with close-ups that feature special amenities and decoration details, the total effect evokes a feeling or mood and completes the experience in the mind of the traveler.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EK9DXB3DNKP9R86GF6WNENBC\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTechnical requirements\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYour photos need to be high-quality to be effectively displayed on different digital platforms. We recommend that all photos:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMeet a minimum resolution of 800 x 600 pixels -- higher resolution is better\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAre in JPG/JPEG format only\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse landscape orientation only, as they will look better on your property page.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAre in color with natural tone\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCome in an original size less than 10MB each\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eLearn even more about taking great property pictures with our Agoda We only allow real guests to review your property after check-out, so that your review score represents an honest and true evaluation of your property’s strengths and weaknesses. Travelers rely on these Review Scores to help make their booking decisions because they trust other travelers, which is why Review Scores are one of the most important factors in getting bookings.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAfter your guests check out, we send them an email inviting them to submit a written review, as well as to grade your property on the factors listed below.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360094263633/mceclip1.png\" categories:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cspan\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eValue for money\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cspan\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eService\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cspan\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFacilities\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cspan\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLocation\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cspan\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCleanliness\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eGuests will rate your property for the above categories on a scale of 1 to 5. We then calculate the average of these overall scores on a 1-10 score and display it as the \u003cstrong\u003eOverall Review Rating\u003c/strong\u003e on your property page. This score will also show up in search results.  \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EK9DDA8AG5SAP4AF2V5ZSBZP\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTips for boosting your Review Score\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMeeting (and exceeding) guests’ expectations \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAccuracy matters -- what you offer on your Agoda listing should exactly match with what you’re going to provide.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThis includes all content data such as facilities, amenities, and photos. Be honest at all times, because dishonesty or even the perception of it will lead to bad reviews.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWhen it comes to service, try to exceed expectations. Guests will frequently compliment service that goes out of its way to do the unexpected.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUpdate your property page regularly \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBy keeping your information updated, you can manage guest expectations ahead of their stay and increase customer satisfaction.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRegularly check the information you provide on YCS. Does it list all your facilities and include updated photos of your property? Are your hotel details up to date? Have you made any improvements or changes in décor that should be shown?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLearn from your current review score \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLook at your current Review Score, and focus on improving the category where you received the lowest score.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRead your existing reviews to see specifics of what guests like, and what they complain about.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor example, if you receive a low Cleanliness rating on your Review Score, and you were able to identify that many guests mention dirty linens, it may be time to replace your bedding, audit your laundry service, or work with housekeeping to ensure all linens are fresher.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOptimize service\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe fastest way to boost your Review Score is to provide excellent service every day, to every guest.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTrain your staff to be attentive, responsive, and have a sense of urgency for every guest’s needs.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRecognize and reward employees who have gone above and beyond for guests, in order to motivate other staff members.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eStaff should always be able to offer a local knowledge of things to do and places to eat. Responsive helpfulness is always memorable to travelers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCleanliness is more important than ever\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnsure your property is well maintained and everything works as it should. Make sure that your staff has the capacity and training to address problems right away, such as minor maintenance problems, water leaks, or loud noises. Guests like a well-run property.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRooms should always be spotless and comfortable, with no clutter.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEstablish a hygiene protocol that is strictly enforced in ways that guests can see. It’s a good idea to make your cleanliness processes public – show them on signage or on a letter to guests in every room.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRead more about \u003cstrong\u003ecleanliness facilities and how to display them \u003c/strong\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/360059929893-Cleanliness-measures-for-your-property\" important?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDQ8BAZQ0NXY5HS6AFGWFDG\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eWhat is content?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt’s all the information in your property listing -- including facilities, amenities, services, reviews, and pictures. Travelers search Agoda every day for their perfect property. The accommodation they choose will most likely be the ones with the content that matches their needs, and what they are looking for in an ideal stay. \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRemember: For travelers, your content IS your property. \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSince most travelers tend to compare similarly priced properties when booking, each property’s content creates perceived value for that same price. Every item you include in your content might make the difference between getting a booking or missing a booking.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDQ8MN8VR8Q3WP0F6MVMKSM\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eWhat is the Content Score?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe Content Score is Agoda’s convenient overall measure of content health for your property listing on Agoda. You can refer to the Content Score at any time as an easy way for you to see if there are any areas where your content is missing and could be improved.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe Content Score is measured by combining 4 elements:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProperty-level content\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRoom-level content\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePhotos\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChild policy\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDQ8T881H3MST5P0ZQGM7HQ\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eProperty-level content\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eProperty level content refers to the common features and offerings of your property that are \u003cstrong\u003eaccessible to\u003c/strong\u003e \u003cstrong\u003eall guests\u003c/strong\u003e, such as swimming pools, fitness facilities, or restaurants. You’re encouraged to fill out and regularly update the information for all the following sections:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHotel Facilities\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan\u003e –\u003c/span\u003e   Research suggests that adding more hotel facilities information can increase your bookings by up to 10%! \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUpdate information about all the facilities and services provided at your property such as restaurants available, Wi-Fi, pet policy, smoking policy, car park, and more.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFind out more about what facilities are most important to travelers \u003cu\u003eHERE\u003c/u\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eLanguages spoken\u003c/span\u003e – Let guests know which languages are spoken by the staff at your property. This is especially important for attracting travelers from other countries. \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eSports and recreation\u003c/span\u003e – Guests love to know what activities they can enjoy while staying at your property.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUpdate information about fitness, swimming pool, and spa facilities.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMention any special sports or activities available.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eUseful information\u003c/span\u003e – fill out other helpful information travelers usually look for.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAirport transfer fee – does your property offer airport transfer? If yes, is it free or charge?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBreakfast fee – Is breakfast offered? Is breakfast free of charge?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck-in and check-out times.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDQ9BB0SSDYS80NHVQCBF73\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eRoom-level content\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRoom level content refers to the features and offerings of your property that are \u003cstrong\u003eavailable in each room type\u003c/strong\u003e. Room facilities, size, view, and bed configuration are key content for each room type. Make sure to update the following information:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eRoom facilities\u003c/span\u003e – Let guests know all facilities provided in the room.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThis includes bathroom amenities like shampoo, toothbrushes, and hairbrushes, as well as mini bar or ironing equipment.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan\u003eRoom details\u003c/span\u003e – Guests want to know more about each room type.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eRoom view \u003c/strong\u003e– Which type of view guests can see out of the window, like lake, beach, nature, ocean, street, pool, park, city?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eRoom size \u003c/strong\u003e– What is the measurement of the room, including the balcony, in square meters?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eBed configuration\u003c/strong\u003e – Which bed types are available in the room --Single bed, king bed, double bed, bunk bed?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDQ9H14F066G58S38GDH3GS\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003ePhotos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePhotos are crucial to your content score, but more importantly they matter to travelers when they’re browsing which hotels to book. You will need:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eHigh quality photos\u003c/strong\u003e, meeting the following guidelines:\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMinimum resolution of 800 x 600\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eJPEG or PNG format only\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLandscape orientation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eColor photos only\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eProperty-level photos \u003c/strong\u003e– we recommend a minimum of 24 photos.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eRoom-level photos \u003c/strong\u003e– we recommend a minimum of 4 photos per room type.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDQ9P514BQ7V4TH3NFAVV1V\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eChild Policy\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYour child policy can add a competitive advantage to your property. It lets guests know who is allowed at your property, and determines which rooms and properties will be shown on the search page when family travelers search for rooms. If your child policy is inaccurately set, potential guests may not even see your rooms or property at all.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDQAY2SWQH59EA5PSZEDTBB\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eWhere can I see my Content Score?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYour Content Score is displayed on your \u003cstrong\u003eProduction Report\u003c/strong\u003e. There, you can see your current content performance and the breakdown of what categories of content should be added to improve the Content Score.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo view your Content Score report…\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDownload the YCS mobile application\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUnder Dashboard tab, click “generate” and “view”\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGo to the last page to see the Content Score Report\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829513/mceclip0.png\" alt=\"mceclip0.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor more information about the Content Score and how to update each content elements, please refer to the \u003ca href=\"https://ycs.agoda.com/content/agoda-content-score-guideline.pdf\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eContent Score Guideline\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDQB7A2ZS184YAAJ6RN1CBH\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eFrequently Asked Questions\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat if I can’t download or view the Content Score on the YCS mobile application?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIf you have difficulties accessing your Content Score report on the mobile application, please contact your market manager and inform them about the issue, or contact the support team via the support button on the YCS website.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan of main photos\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#h_01EFDPSC7TS99H3P5PCNY6THB9\" target=\"_self\"\u003eWhat main photos do I need?\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\n\u003ch1 class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e \u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDPR9D0YW5R3P8X4AXJSY5H\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eWhy photos are important for travelers\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA picture is worth a thousand words, and this is even more true in travel. Travelers use photos to select their destinations, so of course they also rely on photos to choose a hotel room or vacation home. Photos play an important role in creating an attractive and credible property page. Research shows that travelers make up to 60% of their decisions based on photos when browsing which hotels to book. *\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHere’s why else you need a high-quality and complete set of photos for your property:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eInstantly grab traveler’s attention\u003c/strong\u003e. Photos are the most effective way to communicate what your property has to offer to guests in the shortest possible time.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eCreate a first impression\u003c/strong\u003e \u003cstrong\u003ethat sets you apart\u003c/strong\u003e from competitors in your area, making it easier for travelers to remember and choose your property over them.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eIncrease the likelihood of bookings\u003c/strong\u003e. Up to 8x increase in bookings can be gained just from adding more photos! **\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDPREK3K3RJVXVV0FC8V2HD\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eWhich photos do I need for my property?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou should have photos that showcase the facilities, services, and all room types offered on Agoda. We recommend you have both property-level photos and room-level photos.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDPRKGXNJKGRS38Z872MKAW\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eProperty-level photos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eProperty-level photos are photos of the exterior or interior views of your hotel and its facilities. Guests expect to see a realistic representation of your hotel and its location as well as the amenities and services available for them once arrived. These photos also provide the traveler with a sense of “virtual arrival” as they imagine their vacation or business trip.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWe recommend a \u003cstrong\u003eminimum\u003c/strong\u003e of 24 photos, but higher number of photos are highly recommended. The minimum should include at least…\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ex2 photos of the property exterior\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg entrance\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch1 class=\"wysiwyg-indent1\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cimg facilities should include:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eDining facilities\u003c/strong\u003e such as bars, restaurants, coffee shops, or other venues for food and beverages.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084828913/mceclip7.png\" alt=\"mceclip7.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084828933/mceclip8.png\" other appealing and relaxing parts of the property.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg facilities\u003c/strong\u003e such as poolside bar, kids pool, outdoor and indoor pool.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg center.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360083663794/mceclip14.png\" alt=\"mceclip16.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eSports and outdoors facilities\u003c/strong\u003e such as a beach, bicycle rentals, tennis court, squash court, children’s playroom, water activities, golf course, parks, or hiking.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360083663854/mceclip18.png\" alt=\"mceclip18.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360083663874/mceclip19.png\" alt=\"mceclip19.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3 id=\"h_01EFDPRSKT91MB5K8S7N1NBYYZ\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTips on taking facilities photos\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTake outdoor shots during golden hour for a magical quality of light, using shadows and contrasts to enhance the architecture of the building.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTake photos of the property’s exterior and surrounding in wide shots to capture the whole environment of your property’s location.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInterior shots should be taken during the day with as much natural light as possible to achieve soft and bright images.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eShow off your best areas – well-designed lobbies and community areas with distinct or local décor are a major attraction. Remember, guests will want to post pictures of themselves on social media, so these backdrops are important.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDining is key for many travelers. In addition to pictures of bars or restaurants, you may want to include shots of your most picturesque dishes or cocktails. Images of wine cellars, buffets, fresh seafood, or colorful fruit can have wide appeal.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eShow off all your facilities and highlight ones that other hotels might not have. A single facility can make the difference when travelers are making a final decision.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDPRXR1VHCAYKPV5FHS3GYC\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eRoom-level photos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRoom-level photos should capture the room space and its features in a variety of angles to give guests a complete sense of the room’s size, facilities, and view.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWe recommend photographing all room types available at your property with 4-6 photos for each room type. For each room type, it should consist of a \u003cstrong\u003eminimum\u003c/strong\u003e of…\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ex3 photos showcasing the whole room space\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360083663934/mceclip20.png\" alt=\"mceclip20.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829073/mceclip22.png\" alt=\"mceclip22.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829093/mceclip23.png\" alt=\"mceclip23.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ex1 bathroom photo\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829133/mceclip24.png\" alt=\"mceclip24.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePhotos of \u003cstrong\u003eroom features\u003c/strong\u003e could include:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eView\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMini bar\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBalcony or terrace\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSeating areas\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCoffee or tea facilities\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRoom decoration\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePhotos of \u003cstrong\u003ebathrooms facilities\u003c/strong\u003e could include:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBathtub\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBathrobe\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHair dryer\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eComplimentary toiletries\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eTips on taking room-level photos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRooms must be clean, bright and clutter-free before taking any photos. Small details do matter such as wrinkle-free sheets, spotless mirrors, tidy surfaces, emptied trash.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure room is well-lit. Natural lighting during early morning or late afternoon is most ideal when taking room photos. Keep blinds and curtains open and lights on to help further brighten up the room.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTake shots from all four corners to paint a better idea of the entire room layout for guests.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFDPS6V9JCZ0AQ82FGQG6FN5\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eImportance of Main photos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFirst impressions matter, especially the first image a traveler sees of your hotel! The main photo is often the key factor that determines whether travelers will click on your property page on the search page. So it’s very important to carefully choose the main photo that best sells your property’s unique selling points.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"h_01EFDPSC7TS99H3P5PCNY6THB9\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue80\"\u003eWhat main photos do I need?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou need 2 types of main photos…\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eProperty main photo: \u003c/strong\u003ecould be an exterior shot, exceptional interior shot such as a unique key facility.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829153/mceclip25.png\" alt=\"mceclip25.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360084829173/mceclip26.png\" alt=\"mceclip26.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eRoom main photo: \u003c/strong\u003eFor each room type, room main photo is needed. However, we can add new landmarks and essentials if they don't exist in our database. Once added, the system will regenerate the content. We can remove the landmarks displayed here only if they’re permanently closed.\u003cstrong\u003e You can send a request to the Agoda accommodation support team via the Support button in ?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis new setting has been created to address your concerns regarding the limited flexibility of Agoda’s child policy support. This setting allows you to set “free child” limits at the room level.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360034074594/mceclip1.png\"\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis new setting \u003cstrong\u003e\u003cu\u003ereplaces\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e the “Free Child Logic” field and both the “Default free children logic” AND “Respect the number of max allowed guests” settings (shown below).  This field will be removed from the Property Settings section in favor of the MaxAllowedFreeChildren in an effort to provide greater flexibility to child for your property.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01EFNX1NEM4JM7AF43ERQB5MJR\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003eHow do you access the Once in Room Setup, update the “Children allowed for free” field to the desired value for each room:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://agodapropertypartnerhelp.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/360034074634/mceclip3.png\"\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch1 id=\"h_01ECP82JCGS6Q99DGCXT8PCH17\" aria-level=\"1\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"wysiwyg-color-blue90\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFrequently Asked Questions\u003c/strong\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWho does this change impact?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis new setting is available to all properties, however only properties which currently have “children stay free on existing bedding” enabled will see any noticeable differences as part of the update.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHow does this setting work?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eProperties will now be able to indicate exactly how many children can stay for free at the room level. To do this, update the Children allowed for free to the desired value. Note, child guests in excess of this value will be treated as adult guests and subject to standard room occupancy constraints.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4 id=\"h_01EFNX2AAQJ1B3FD7KZKG2HPD2\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy is this good for my property?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis setting will allow properties to customize the maximum number of “free” children per each room – and avoid situations where a guest arrives with too many children.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat updates are happening?\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe following settings will be updated only if you currently have enabled “children stay free on existing bedding”:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe “Free Children Logic” setting will be replaced with Children allowed for free\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe Children allowed for free value will be updated based on your current settings\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSettings that prevent family bookings will be updated (for example, the “Minimum Guest Age” will be updated to “0”\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOther minor visual / aesthetic changes will be made\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat if I don’t want to allow children to stay for
